Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 45/2 (AKA Manche45 revision 2), the final, flown mission release of the Apollo 10 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software. Comanche 45/2 was preceded by Comanche 44 and Comanche 45. The reconstruction is believed to be exactly accurate, but in the absence of an actual Apollo-era listing of Comanche 45/2, some explanation of the reconstruction process is needed to insure confidence in that accuracy.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 45 (itself previously accurately reconstructed). Comanche 45 source code was then modified by incorporating changes known from contemporary documentation to have been made between revisions 45 and 45/2. The now-reconstructed Comanche 45/2 source code was verified by assembling it and checking that the assembled code had the expected known-correct memory-bank checksums. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code tend to match those in the Comanche 55, the most-similar revision of Comanche for which we have access to an actual non-reconstructed hardcopy; the source code would likely have different page numbers in a contemporary Comanche 45 listing.

Annotations that were not present in the contemporary source code have been added to the reconstructed code to justify each change relative to Comanche 44. Here's a guide to the Apollo documentation referenced in those annotations:
  • MIT/IL engineering drawing 2021153D, sheet 3. Listing of the memory-bank checksums for Comanche 45.
  • Reconstructed Comanche 45 (Apollo 10 CM second release) assembly listing.
  • Reconstructed Comanche 51 (Apollo 11 CM initial release) assembly listing.
  • Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, p. 91.
Comments expected to have been present in the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub repository. 

001576,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001577,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001578,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Manche45 revision 2.
001579,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
001580,000006:                                                                                                  ##              final, flown release of the flight software for the Command
001581,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10.
001582,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
001583,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001584,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Manche 45/2 in NASA drawing
001585,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
001586,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
001587,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001588,000014:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001589,000015:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001590,000016:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-12-24 MAS  Created from Comanche 45, and added the new
001591,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              padloads needed for the R-2 potential model.
001592,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2020-12-24 RSB  Added or beefed up reconstruction-justifying
001593,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              annotations.
001594,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2021-05-30 ABS  Fixed R53FLBIT value to be BIT6.
001595,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              Various symbol name fixes.
001596,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Added V96ONBIT definition present in Comanche 55 scans.

001600,000026:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001601,000027: 
001602,000028:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001603,000029:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001604,000030:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001605,000031: 
001606,000032:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001607,000033:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001608,000034:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001609,000035: 
001610,000036:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001611,000037:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001612,000038:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001613,000039: 
001614,000040:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001615,000041:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001616,000042: 
001617,000043:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001618,000044: 
001619,000045:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001620,000046:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001621,000047: 
001622,000048:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001623,000049: 
001624,000050:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001625,000051:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001626,000052: 
001627,000053:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001628,000054:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001629,000055:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001630,000056:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001631,000057:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001632,000058:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001633,000059: 
001634,000060:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001635,000061: 
001636,000062:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001637,000063:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001638,000064:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001639,000065:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001640,000066:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001641,000067:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001642,000068:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001643,000069:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001644,000070:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001645,000071:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001646,000072:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 38 

001648,000074:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001649,000075:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001650,000076:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001651,000077:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001652,000078:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001653,000079:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001654,000080:

001658,000084: 
001659,000085: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001660,000086: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001661,000087: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001662,000088: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001663,000089: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001664,000090: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001665,000091: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001666,000092:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001667,000093: 
001668,000094: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001669,000095: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001670,000096: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001671,000097: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001672,000098: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001673,000099: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001674,000100: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001675,000101: 
001676,000102: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20
